jor_tail,233,41,3	script	Shufapa#ep21ex01	4_EP19_IWIN_DIVER,{
	if(isbegin_quest(18233) < 2){
		npctalk "Shufapa : The water was cold again today...","",bc_self;
		end;
	}
	if(BaseLevel < 230){
		mes "[Shufapa]";
		mes "I've been feeling something strange over there lately.";
		mes "That place is the Scale Island, I'm thinking of going there soon.";
		next;
		mes "^4D4DFFThis quest is only for those who are level 230 or above.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if(isbegin_quest(18233) == 2 && isbegin_quest(18334) == 0){
		cutin "ep19_iwin_diver02.png",2;
		mes "[Shufapa]";
		mes "Oh, adventurer.";
		mes "You came just in time.";
		mes "Just wait a moment, the others will also be here soon.";
		next;
		select("What's going on?");
		cutin "ep19_iwin_diver01.png",2;
		mes "[Shufapa]";
		mes "Huh? Didn't you hear? We were planning to go investigate the tiny island over there called the Scale Island.";
		mes "Adventurer, aren't you going to come with us?";
		next;
		cloaknpc("Nillem#ep21nlm01",false,getcharid(0));
		cloaknpc("Aurelie#ep21orl01",false,getcharid(0));
		cloaknpc("Lehar#ep21rhr01",false,getcharid(0));
		cutin "ep19_lehar01.png",2;
		mes "[Lehar]";
		mes "Oh, adventurer! Percect timing, I was just about to come and find you.";
		mes "We are going to the Scale Island, you should come with us!";
		next;
		cutin "ep172_nillem01.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "Oh, dear customer~ Is that really you?";
		mes "I've always provided you the teleport services from the Cat on a Bullet, aren't you happy to see me?";
		next;
		select("Nillem, why are you here?");
		cutin "ep172_nillem02.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "I'm here because you need me for various reasons, maybe?";
		mes "Haha, after the dimensional rift occured, various things were going here and there, right?";
		next;
		cutin "ep172_nillem02.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "It's difficult to respond on time if a rift or a similar phenomena suddenly occured, that's why I did some research to predict where it will occur.";
		next;
		cutin "ep172_nillem03.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "Who am I? I am the genius wizard Nillem-☆";
		mes "But why you asked? It's for the sake of my dear customer who works tirelessly for the safety of the continent, isn't that obvious?";
		next;
		cutin "ep19_lehar07.png",2;
		mes "[Lehar]";
		mes "Eh.... Are you serious. Simply for that.";
		next;
		cutin "ep172_nillem01.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "Of course, what do you think I do? Anyways, I came here because I detected a similar mana wavelength when the rift occured.";
		mes "Entering the rumored Isgard, and meeting the rumored guardians...!";
		next;
		cutin "ep19_aurelie02.png",0;
		mes "[Aurelie]";
		mes "Can we end the greetings and go?";
		mes "The mana wavelength of that place is unusual.";
		mes "We need to check if it's related to the barrier's seal.";
		next;
		cutin "ep19_lehar01.png",2;
		mes "[Lehar]";
		mes "Yes. Shall we go now?";
		mes "Wizard. Is that the place where you felt the wavelength?";
		next;
		cutin "ep172_nillem02.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "Correct. Leon and Aurelie also confirmed it a while ago back in the Ice Castle.";
		mes "Are we not going?";
		next;
		select("Aren't you going to ask my opinion?");
		cutin "ep172_nillem03.png",1;
		mes "[Nillem]";
		mes "Come on~ There is no need to ask. I already the know the answer.";
		mes "This is something urgent, we can take care of it now and think about it later. Let's go now~. Let's go quickly~☆";
		next;
		cutin "ep19_iwin_diver02.png",2;
		mes "[Shufapa]";
		mes "Shall we go to the Scale Island?";
		mes "Should we leave now?";
		setquest 18334;
		close2;
		pcblock(true);
		cutin "",255;
		npctalk "Finally.","Nillem#ep21nlm01",bc_self;
		npctalk "Please.","Aurelie#ep21orl01",bc_self;
		npctalk "Let's go!","Lehar#ep21rhr01",bc_self;
		sleep2 1000;
		cloaknpc("Nillem#ep21nlm01",true,getcharid(0));
		cloaknpc("Aurelie#ep21orl01",true,getcharid(0));
		cloaknpc("Lehar#ep21rhr01",true,getcharid(0));
        npctalk "Shufapa : How about you?","",bc_self;
		pcblock(false);
        if(select("I'll go now.","I'll go later.") == 2)
        	npctalk "I'll be here for a while, just let me know when you want to go to Scale Island.","",bc_self;
		else {
			npctalk "Shufapa : Let's go.","",bc_self;
			warp "jor_crk",137,137;
		}
		end;
	}
	cutin "ep19_iwin_diver02.png",2;
	mes "[Shufapa]";
    mes "Are you going to Scale Island?";
	next;
	if(select("Go to Scale Island.","No.") == 2){
	    mes "[Shufapa]";
	    mes "I'll be here for a while, just let me know when you want to go to Scale Island.";
	    close3;
    } else {
		cutin "",255;
		npctalk "Shufapa : Let's go.","",bc_self;
		warp "jor_crk",137,137;
	}
	end;

OnInit:
    questinfo QTYPE_QUEST,QMARK_YELLOW,"BaseLevel >= 230 && isbegin_quest(18233) == 2 && isbegin_quest(18334) == 0";
end;
}

jor_crk,139,141,3	script	Shufapa#ep21ex02	4_EP19_IWIN_DIVER,{
	mes "[Shufapa]";
	mes "Are you finish investigating? Do you want to go return?";
	mes "To the airship? Ice Castle? Where do you want to go?";
	cutin "ep19_iwin_diver02.png",2;
	next;
	switch(select("To the airship.","To Ice Castle.","I'm staying.")){
		case 1:
			mes "[Shufapa]";
			mes "I'll take you near the airship.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			warp "jor_tail",232,43;
			end;

		case 2:
			mes "[Shufapa]";
			mes "I'll take you near the Ice Castle.";
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			warp "icecastle",145,85;
			end;

		case 3:
			mes "[Shufapa]";
			mes "Okay. I'll wait here.";
			close3;
	}
	end;
}

function	script	ep21_clean_check	{
	for(.@i = 16806; .@i <= 16809; .@i++)
		if(isbegin_quest(.@i) != 2) return false;
	return true;
}

jor_mbase,207,192,3	duplicate(dummynpc)	Tan#ep21tan01	4_EP21_TAN

function	script	ep21_witness_check	{
	for(.@i = 18339; .@i <= 18341; .@i++)
		if(isbegin_quest(.@i) != 1)	return false;
	return true;
}

function	script	hasUnlockedHard	{
	for(.@i = 13; .@i <= 19; .@i++){
		if(get_reputation_points(.@i) < 1000)
			return false;
	}
	return true;
}

luna_sf2,260,46,4	script(CLOAKED)	Heine#md2	4_EP21_HEINE_TAB,{
	if(isbegin_quest(18360) < 2) end;
	.@bool = hasUnlockedHard();
	switch(checkquest(12647,PLAYTIME)){
		case -1:
			.@normal = true;
			break;
		case 0:
		case 1:
			if(!.@bool){
				mes "^0000ffEveryone is not moving as if they’re frozen in place. Could time have momentarily stopped?^000000";
				close;
			} else
				.@cd += 1;
			break;
		case 2:
			erasequest 12674;
			.@normal = true;
			break;
	}
	switch(checkquest(12648,PLAYTIME)){
		case -1:
			.@hard = true;
			break;
		case 0:
		case 1:
			if(.@cd){
				mes "^0000ffEveryone is not moving as if they’re frozen in place. Could time have momentarily stopped?^000000";
				close;
			} else
				.@cd += 1;
			break;
		case 2:
			.@hard = true;
			erasequest 12648;
			break;
	}
	if(.@cd == 2){
		mes "^0000ffEveryone is not moving as if they’re frozen in place. Could time have momentarily stopped?^000000";
		close;
	}
	cutin "ep21_ilse_heine02.png",2;
	mes "[Heine]";
	mes "Hehe, this is the perfect time to showcase my life's work, my spacial magic, then Hopi-hop Spacial Jump.";
	close2;
	cutin "",255;
	.@party_id = getcharid(1);
	if(!.@party_id){
		mes "^0000ffPlease speak to me once the party leader has finished the preparation to enter.^000000";
		close;
	}
	npctalk "Hm. I feel like I've heard that before.","Tan#md",bc_self;
	npctalk "I'm feeling the same as well.","",bc_self;
	cutin "",255;
	if(is_party_leader() && instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) != "Final Battle(Normal)" && instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) != "Final Battle(Hard)"){
		if(select((.@normal == true ? "Prepare for Final Battle(Normal)" : ""),(.@bool == true && .@hard == true ? "Prepare for Final Battle(Hard)" : "")) == 1)
			.@md_name$ = "Final Battle(Normal)";
		else
			.@md_name$ = "Final Battle(Hard)";
		if(instance_create(.@md_name$) == -3)
			instance_warning(2,.@md_name$);
		end;
	}
	if(instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) != "Final Battle(Normal)" && instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) != "Final Battle(Hard)"){
		mes "^0000ffPlease speak to me once the party leader has finished the preparation to enter.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if(instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) == "Final Battle(Normal)"){
		select("Begin the Final Battle(Normal)");
		.@md_name$ = "Final Battle(Normal)";
		if(instance_enter(.@md_name$) != IE_OK){
			mes "^0000ffPlease speak to me once the party leader has finished the preparation to enter.^000000";
			close;
		}
		setquest 12647;
		mapannounce "luna_sf2", "The adventurer, " + strcharinfo(0) + " is entering the Final Battle(Normal).", bc_map, "0x00FFAA";
		end;
	}
	if(instance_live_info(ILI_NAME,instance_id(IM_PARTY)) == "Final Battle(Hard)"){
		if(isbegin_quest(12650) < 2){
			mes "^0000ffPlease speak to me once the party leader has finished the preparation to enter.^000000";
			close;
		}
		select("Begin the Final Battle(Hard)");
		.@md_name$ = "Final Battle(Hard)";
		if(instance_enter(.@md_name$) != IE_OK){
			mes "^0000ffPlease speak to me once the party leader has finished the preparation to enter.^000000";
			close;
		}
		setquest 12648;
		mapannounce "luna_sf2", "The adventurer, " + strcharinfo(0) + " is entering the Final Battle(Normal).", bc_map, "0x00FFAA";
		end;

function	fishing_cutins	{
	.@current = getarg(1);
	for(.@i = 0; .@i < getarg(0); .@i++){
		sleep2 400;
		if((.@current % 2) + .@i)
			cutin "2013_summer_fish_3.bmp",2;
		else
			cutin "2013_summer_fish_4.bmp",2;
	}
	return (.@i % 2) + 3;
}

OnInit:
	questinfo QTYPE_CLICKME,QMARK_YELLOW,"isbegin_quest(19200) == 1";
end;
}
